STEP 3: THE WORKER CODE (worker.py)
This is the logic that runs on the Dell. It polls for missions, browses the web using your residential IP, and updates Firestore with the results.

Create the file:

Bash
nano worker.py
Paste this code:

Python
import os
import time
import json
import logging
import random
from google.cloud import firestore
from playwright.async_api import async_playwright
from fake_useragent import UserAgent
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
import asyncio

# SETUP LOGGING
logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format='%(asctime)s - [KAJI-WORKER] - %(levelname)s - %(message)s'
)
logger = logging.getLogger("KajiWorker")

# CONFIG
PROJECT_ID = "veiled-vector-core"
CREDENTIALS_PATH = "credentials.json"
os.environ["GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS"] = CREDENTIALS_PATH

# INIT FIRESTORE
db = firestore.Client()
ua = UserAgent()

async def scrape_target(url: str):
    """
    Scrapes a target URL using the Residential IP (No Proxy needed).
    """
    logger.info(f"Launching Browser for: {url}")
    async with async_playwright() as p:
        # Launch standard Chromium (Headless)
        # No proxy args needed because we ARE the residential node.
        browser = await p.chromium.launch(headless=True)
        
        # Generate Fake Identity
        try:
            random_ua = ua.random
        except:
            random_ua = "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/120.0.0.0 Safari/537.36"
            
        context = await browser.new_context(
            user_agent=random_ua,
            viewport={"width": 1920, "height": 1080},
            permissions=["geolocation"]
        )
        
        # Anti-Detection Scripts
        await context.add_init_script("Object.defineProperty(navigator, 'webdriver', {get: () => undefined})")
        
        page = await context.new_page()
        
        try:
            # Go to Page
            await page.goto(url, timeout=90000, wait_until="domcontentloaded")
            
            # Random wait to look human (3-7 seconds)
            await page.wait_for_timeout(random.randint(3000, 7000))
            
            # Extract Content
            content = await page.content()
            title = await page.title()
            
            # Clean HTML (Save bandwidth)
            soup = BeautifulSoup(content, 'html.parser')
            for script in soup(["script", "style", "svg", "path", "noscript"]):
                script.extract()
            clean_text = soup.get_text(separator=' | ', strip=True)[:50000] # Cap at 50k chars
            
            await browser.close()
            return {"status": "SUCCESS", "title": title, "data": clean_text}
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Scrape Error: {e}")
            await browser.close()
            return {"status": "FAILED", "error": str(e)}

async def process_mission(doc):
    """
    Handles a single mission from the queue.
    """
    mission_data = doc.to_dict()
    task = mission_data.get("task")
    mission_id = doc.id
    
    logger.info(f"Received Mission {mission_id}: {task}")
    
    # 1. Update Status to IN_PROGRESS
    doc.reference.update({"status": "IN_PROGRESS", "worker": "KAJI_DELL"})
    
    # 2. Extract URL (Basic Logic)
    target_url = next((word for word in task.split() if word.startswith("http")), None)
    
    # If no URL, default to a search (DuckDuckGo HTML)
    if not target_url:
        logger.info("No URL found. Defaulting to Search...")
        target_url = f"https://html.duckduckgo.com/html/?q={task}"
    
    # 3. Execute Scrape
    result = await scrape_target(target_url)
    
    # 4. Report Back
    if result["status"] == "SUCCESS":
        logger.info(f"Mission {mission_id} SUCCESS. Uploading Data...")
        doc.reference.update({
            "status": "COMPLETED",
            "result_title": result["title"],
            "result_data": result["data"],
            "completed_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP
        })
    else:
        logger.warning(f"Mission {mission_id} FAILED.")
        doc.reference.update({
            "status": "FAILED",
            "error": result["error"],
            "completed_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP
        })

async def main_loop():
    logger.info("KAJI WORKER ONLINE. Waiting for missions...")
    
    while True:
        # Poll Firestore for 'PENDING' missions
        # We limit to 1 to process sequentially
        docs = db.collection("mission_queue").where("status", "==", "PENDING").limit(1).stream()
        
        found_task = False
        for doc in docs:
            found_task = True
            await process_mission(doc)
        
        if not found_task:
            # Sleep to save CPU/Bandwidth if no work
            time.sleep(5)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(main_loop())

#!/bin/bash

# ==========================================
# VEILED VECTOR INC. - CLOUD DB ALIGNMENT
# ==========================================
# Objective: Point Cloud Brain to 'veiled-vector-core-firestore'
# Target: veiled-vector-orchestrator

PROJECT_ID="veiled-vector-core"
SERVICE_NAME="veiled-vector-orchestrator"
REGION="us-central1"
DB_NAME="veiled-vector-core-firestore"

echo "VECTOR_LOG: Aligning Cloud Brain to Database '$DB_NAME'..."

cd veiled-vector-cloud

# 1. REWRITE DSIE CORE (With Correct DB ID)
cat <<EOF > src/dsie_core.py
import logging
import google.generativeai as genai
from google.cloud import firestore
import os
import json
import datetime

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")

# CONNECT TO SPECIFIC DATABASE
try:
    db = firestore.Client(database="${DB_NAME}")
except Exception as e:
    logger.error(f"Failed to connect to DB: {e}")
    # Fallback to default if specific fails (safety net)
    db = firestore.Client()

class DSIECore:
    def __init__(self):
        self.api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY")
        if self.api_key:
            genai.configure(api_key=self.api_key)
            # Using the hardcoded stable model
            self.model = genai.GenerativeModel('gemini-2.0-flash-001')

    async def run_cycle(self, task: str):
        logger.info(f"DELEGATING MISSION: {task}")
        
        mission_id = f"mission_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d%H%M%S')}"
        
        # Write to the Mission Queue
        doc_ref = db.collection("mission_queue").document(mission_id)
        doc_ref.set({
            "task": task,
            "status": "PENDING",
            "created_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP,
            "worker": "KAJI_DELL",
            "target_db": "${DB_NAME}"
        })
        
        logger.info(f"Mission {mission_id} queued for Kaji.")
        return {"status": "Delegated to Dell", "mission_id": mission_id, "database": "${DB_NAME}"}
EOF

echo "VECTOR_LOG: Code Patched."

# 2. REDEPLOY
echo "VECTOR_LOG: Re-deploying Cloud Orchestrator..."
gcloud builds submit --tag gcr.io/$PROJECT_ID/$SERVICE_NAME

gcloud run deploy $SERVICE_NAME \
  --image gcr.io/$PROJECT_ID/$SERVICE_NAME \
  --platform managed \
  --region $REGION \
  --allow-unauthenticated \
  --memory 512Mi \
  --cpu 1 \
  --service-account vector-archivist@$PROJECT_ID.iam.gserviceaccount.com \
  --set-secrets="GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY=GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY:latest"

echo "=========================================="
echo "VEILED VECTOR: CLOUD DB ALIGNED"
echo "=========================================="

1. Create the Script
In Cloud Shell (Galaxy Book):

Bash
nano deploy_v5_analyst.sh
2. Paste the Code
(This restores the Brain/Drive logic but points it at Firestore data instead of live scraping).

Bash
#!/bin/bash

# ==========================================
# VEILED VECTOR INC. - v5.1 ANALYST UPGRADE
# ==========================================
# Objective: Enable Cloud Brain to process Kaji's results
# Target: veiled-vector-orchestrator

PROJECT_ID="veiled-vector-core"
SERVICE_NAME="veiled-vector-orchestrator"
REGION="us-central1"

echo "VECTOR_LOG: Upgrading Brain to Analyst Mode..."

cd veiled-vector-cloud

# 1. REWRITE DSIE CORE (Dispatcher + Analyst)
cat <<EOF > src/dsie_core.py
import logging
import google.generativeai as genai
from google.generativeai.types import HarmCategory, HarmBlockThreshold
from google.cloud import firestore
import os
import json
import re
import datetime
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
from src.tools.drive import DriveClient

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")
db = firestore.Client(database="veiled-vector-core-firestore")

class DSIECore:
    def __init__(self):
        self.api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY")
        if self.api_key:
            genai.configure(api_key=self.api_key)
            # Use the verified stable model
            self.model = genai.GenerativeModel('gemini-2.0-flash-001')
        self.drive = None
        
        # Safety: BLOCK_NONE for gambling content
        self.safety = {
            HarmCategory.HARM_CATEGORY_HARASSMENT: HarmBlockThreshold.BLOCK_NONE,
            HarmCategory.HARM_CATEGORY_HATE_SPEECH: HarmBlockThreshold.BLOCK_NONE,
            HarmCategory.HARM_CATEGORY_SEXUALLY_EXPLICIT: HarmBlockThreshold.BLOCK_NONE,
            HarmCategory.HARM_CATEGORY_DANGEROUS_CONTENT: HarmBlockThreshold.BLOCK_NONE,
        }

    def extract_json(self, text):
        match = re.search(r'\{.*\}', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match: return json.loads(match.group(0))
        match_list = re.search(r'\[.*\]', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match_list: return json.loads(match_list.group(0))
        raise ValueError("No JSON object found in LLM response")

    async def run_cycle(self, task: str):
        """ DISPATCHER: Sends task to Dell """
        logger.info(f"DELEGATING MISSION: {task}")
        mission_id = f"mission_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d%H%M%S')}"
        doc_ref = db.collection("mission_queue").document(mission_id)
        doc_ref.set({
            "task": task,
            "status": "PENDING",
            "created_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP,
            "worker": "KAJI_DELL",
            "target_db": "veiled-vector-core-firestore"
        })
        return {"status": "Delegated to Dell", "mission_id": mission_id}

    async def process_pending_results(self):
        """ ANALYST: Checks for completed work and finalizes it """
        logger.info("Checking for completed missions...")
        # Find missions that are COMPLETED by Dell but not yet ANALYZED
        docs = db.collection("mission_queue").where("status", "==", "COMPLETED").stream()
        
        processed_count = 0
        if not self.drive: self.drive = DriveClient()

        for doc in docs:
            data = doc.to_dict()
            if data.get("analysis_status") == "DONE":
                continue # Skip already processed
            
            mission_id = doc.id
            logger.info(f"Processing Results for {mission_id}...")
            
            # 1. Get HTML from Firestore
            html_content = data.get("result_data", "")
            task = data.get("task", "")
            
            # 2. Analyze with Gemini
            try:
                prompt = f"""
                Analyze this raw HTML data.
                Task: {task}
                Extract the relevant odds/data into valid JSON.
                HTML Content: {html_content[:30000]}
                """
                response = self.model.generate_content(prompt, safety_settings=self.safety)
                parsed_data = self.extract_json(response.text)
                
                # 3. Upload to Drive
                filename = f"{mission_id}_results.json"
                self.drive.upload_json(filename, parsed_data)
                
                # 4. Mark Done
                doc.reference.update({
                    "analysis_status": "DONE",
                    "final_file": filename,
                    "analyzed_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP
                })
                processed_count += 1
                logger.info(f"Mission {mission_id} Analyzed & Saved.")
                
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Analysis Failed for {mission_id}: {e}")
                doc.reference.update({"analysis_status": "FAILED", "error": str(e)})

        return {"status": "Batch Complete", "processed": processed_count}
EOF

# 2. UPDATE MAIN (Add Process Endpoint)
cat <<EOF > src/main.py
from fastapi import FastAPI, BackgroundTasks, Header, HTTPException
from pydantic import BaseModel
from src.dsie_core import DSIECore
import os

app = FastAPI(title="Veiled Vector Orchestrator")
brain = DSIECore()
VECTOR_API_KEY = "buffalo-bills-mafia-secret"

class Mission(BaseModel):
    task: str

@app.post("/mission")
async def launch_mission(mission: Mission, x_vector_key: str = Header(None)):
    if x_vector_key != VECTOR_API_KEY: raise HTTPException(403, "Unauthorized")
    return await brain.run_cycle(mission.task)

@app.post("/process")
async def process_results(background_tasks: BackgroundTasks, x_vector_key: str = Header(None)):
    if x_vector_key != VECTOR_API_KEY: raise HTTPException(403, "Unauthorized")
    background_tasks.add_task(brain.process_pending_results)
    return {"status": "Processing Started"}
EOF

echo "VECTOR_LOG: Re-deploying Analyst..."
gcloud builds submit --tag gcr.io/$PROJECT_ID/$SERVICE_NAME

gcloud run deploy $SERVICE_NAME \
  --image gcr.io/$PROJECT_ID/$SERVICE_NAME \
  --platform managed \
  --region $REGION \
  --allow-unauthenticated \
  --memory 1Gi \
  --cpu 1 \
  --service-account vector-archivist@$PROJECT_ID.iam.gserviceaccount.com \
  --set-secrets="GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY=GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY:latest,DRIVE_SERVICE_ACCOUNT_KEY=DRIVE_SERVICE_ACCOUNT_KEY:latest"

echo "=========================================="
echo "VEILED VECTOR: ANALYST ONLINE"
echo "=========================================="
3. Execute
Save and run:

Bash
chmod +x deploy_v5_analyst.sh
./deploy_v5_analyst.sh
THE FINAL STEP: HARVEST
Once "VEILED VECTOR: ANALYST ONLINE" appears:

Run this command to trigger the Cloud Brain to look at what Kaji (The Dell) just uploaded.

Bash
SERVICE_URL="YOUR_SERVICE_URL_HERE"

curl -X POST "$SERVICE_URL/process" \
     -H "x-vector-key: buffalo-bills-mafia-secret"
Expectation:

The API returns {"status": "Processing Started"}.

The Brain reads the HTML from Firestore (the one Kaji just uploaded).

Gemini extracts the odds.

mission_2025..._results.json appears in your Google Drive.

Report back with: "File Secured in Drive."
